class=\"clearfix\"></div>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\tApril 21, 2017\t\t\t<span class=\"by-author\"> by <span class=\"author vcard\"><a class=\"url fn n\" data-url=\"https://www.sqlshack.com/sql-server-vnext-microsoft-love-linux/\"><div class=\"atclear\"></div></div><h2>Introduction</h2>\n<p>\n  In the 90s and at the beginning of the 21 century, Linux and Windows were decidedly working at cross purposes\n</p>\n<p>\n  However, starting on 2009, Microsoft started to contribute with code in the Linux Kernel. On 2013, Azure supported Virtual Machines in Ubuntu and later came the support to .NET in Linux, Visual Studio for Linux, PowerShell in Linux, support to monitor Linux server to monitor in SCOM (<a href=\"https://technet.microsoft.com/en-us/library/hh212754(v=sc.12).aspx\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow\">System Center Operation Manager</a>) and now, the support for SQL Server that is on the previous version when this article was published and it is planned to be released this year (2017). Microsoft is a Platinum member of the Linux Foundation now.\n</p> <a href=\"https://www.sqlshack.com/sql-server-vnext-microsoft-love-linux/\" class=\"more-link\">Read more »</a><!-- AddThis Sharing Buttons below --><div class=\"at-below-post-homepage addthis_default_style addthis_toolbox at-wordpress-hide\" data-url=\"https://www.sqlshack.com/sql-server-vnext-microsoft-love-linux/\"><div class=\"atclear\"></div></div>\t\t\t\n\t\t</div><!-- .entry-content -->\n\n\t\t\n\n\n\t\t<footer class=\"entry-meta\">\n\n\t\t\t<a href=\"https://www.sqlshack.com/sql-server-2017/\" rel=\"category tag\">SQL Server 2017</a>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\n\t\t</footer><!-- .entry-meta -->\n\t\t\n\t\t</div><!-- .home-post -->\n\n\t</article><!-- #post -->\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\n\n\t<article id=\"post-16013\" class=\"post-16013 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-sql-database-development\">\n\t\t<div class=\"avatar\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"avatar-big-picture\"> \n\t\t\t\t\t<img src=\"/wp-content/uploads/2014/08/sifiso_ndlovu_80x80.png\" alt=\"Sifiso W. Such a decision affected development teams that uses Team Explorer to store, collaborate and manage SQL Server-related solutions (i.e. T-SQL scripts, SSRS, SSAS, SSIS) into TFS source control. Well, the good news is that it looks like Microsoft has finally heeded the call of bringing back the standalone installer for Team Explorer as <em>Visual Studio 2017</em> (available from release <a href=\"https://www.visualstudio.com/en-us/news/releasenotes/vs2017-relnotes\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow\"><em>26403.00</em></a>) now contains a standalone <em>Team Explorer 2017</em> installer.\n</p> <a href=\"https://www.sqlshack.com/return-standalone-installer-team-explorer-2017/\" class=\"more-link\">Read more »</a><!-- AddThis Sharing Buttons below --><div problem with parallelism</a>\n\n\t\t\t</h1>\n\t\t\t<div class=\"clearfix\"></div>\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\tApril 13, 2017\t\t\t<span class=\"by-author\"> by <span class=\"author vcard\"><a class=\"url fn n\" href=\"https://www.sqlshack.com/author/neeraj/\" rel=\"author\">Neeraj Prasad Sharma</a></span></span>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\n\n\t\t</header><!-- .entry-header -->\n\n\n\n\t\t\n\t\t<div class=\"entry-content\">\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- AddThis Sharing Buttons above --><div class=\"at-above-post-homepage addthis_default_style addthis_toolbox at-wordpress-hide\" data-url=\"https://www.sqlshack.com/sql-server-top-clause-performance-problem-parallelism/\"><div class=\"atclear\"></div></div><h2>\n   Basics of TOP Operator\n</h2>\n<p>\n  The TOP keyword in SQL Server is a non-ANSI standard expression to limit query results to some set of pre-specified rows. <span style=\"background-color: #d9d9d9\">As an argument, it takes 0 to positive Bigint (9223372036854775807) and anything beyond or less gives an error message.</span> TOP without an order by clause, in production, seems buggy because it can produce results in any order depending on the current schema and execution plan. You can also specify a percent with TOP expression which returns only the expression percent of rows from the result set. Float expressions used in TOP percent are rounded up to the next integer value. \n</p> <a href=\"https://www.sqlshack.com/sql-server-top-clause-performance-problem-parallelism/\" class=\"more-link\">Read more »</a><!-- AddThis Sharing Buttons below --><div class=\"at-below-post-homepage addthis_default_style addthis_toolbox at-wordpress-hide\" <a href=\"/what-is-a-sql-server-deadlock/\"> What is a SQL Server Deadlock</a> and <a href=\"/understanding-graphical-representation-sql-server-deadlock-graph/\"> Understanding the graphical representation of the SQL Server Deadlock Graph</a>, I discussed what a deadlock is, how SQL Server handles deadlocks, some tips on how to reduce deadlocks and ultimately what information you can glean by just looking at the graphical representation of the Deadlock Graph. \n</p>\n<p>\n  In this article, I will look at what information is available in the XML description of the Deadlock Graph. The XML contains information which is not visible in the graphical representation of the Deadlock Graph, which makes it necessary for us to look at the XML description. \n</p> <a
